// Ohmpilot is off at this point, communication from Gen24 is directed at BYD battery which is also supposed go on Modbus 0 with ID x15 (21 decimal)
// it seems the Gen24 is polling for a response every minute on the Modbus link 
// The Modbus was sniffed with Serial Port monitor from /www.eltima.com using a RS485 to USB dongle
// Timed communication dump in HEX bytes with ASCII translation in the second column
// I noticed occasional extra 00 bytes just after CRC values in the communication otherwise it is fairly clear
// Please note that not all send/receive interactions are separated by lines with time, it is just what the software produces (raw file)
//===================================================================
